    <ol start="2">
     <li>
      <p>
       对于所有N个样本，似然函数为：
      </p>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          L 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           w 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           = 
          
          
          
            ∏ 
           
           
           
             n 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            N 
           
          
          
          
            1 
           
           
            
            
              2 
             
            
              π 
             
            
              β 
             
            
           
          
         
           exp 
          
         
           ⁡ 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           − 
          
          
           
           
             ( 
            
            
            
              y 
             
             
             
               ( 
              
             
               n 
              
             
               ) 
              
             
            
           
             − 
            
            
            
              w 
             
            
              T 
             
            
            
            
              x 
             
             
             
               ( 
              
             
               n 
              
             
               ) 
              
             
            
            
            
              ) 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
           
           
             2 
            
           
             β 
            
           
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          L(w) = \prod_{n=1}^N \frac{1}{\sqrt{2\pi\beta}}\exp(-\frac{(y^{(n)}-w^Tx^{(n)})^2}{2\beta})
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            L
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
            w
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            =
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.6997em; vertical-align: -0.538em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mop">
            <span class="mop op-symbol small-op" style="position: relative; top: 0em;">
             ∏
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.9812em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.4003em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    n
                   </span>
                   <span class="mrel mtight">
                    =
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    1
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.2029em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
                   N
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2997em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
            </span>
            <span class="mfrac">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8451em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.6016em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord sqrt mtight">
                    <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                     <span class="vlist-r">
                      <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8406em;">
                       <span class="svg-align" style="top: -3em;">
                        <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                        </span>
                        <span class="mord mtight" style="padding-left: 0.833em;">
                         <span class="mord mtight">

     <li>
      <p>
       对
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          w 
          
         
        
          w
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
            w
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
       求导并令其为0：
      </p>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          ∂ 
            
           
             ln 
            
           
             ⁡ 
            
           
             L 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             w 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
           
           
             ∂ 
            
           
             w 
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
          
          
            1 
           
          
            β 
           
          
          
          
            ∑ 
           
           
           
             n 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            N 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            y 
           
           
           
             ( 
            
           
             n 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
           − 
          
          
          
            w 
           
          
            T 
           
          
          
          
            x 
           
           
           
             ( 
            
           
             n 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
           ) 
          
          
          
            x 
           
           
           
             ( 
            
           
             n 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          \frac{\partial \ln L(w)}{\partial w} = \frac{1}{\beta}\sum_{n=1}^N(y^{(n)}-w^Tx^{(n)})x^{(n)} = 0
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.355em; vertical-align: -0.345em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
            </span>
            <span class="mfrac">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.01em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.655em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0556em;">
                    ∂
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
                    w
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.23em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;">
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.485em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0556em;">
                    ∂
                   </span>
                   <span class="mspace mtight" style="margin-right: 0.1952em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="mop mtight">
                    <span class="mtight">
                     l
                    </span>
                    <span class="mtight">
                     n
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span class="mspace mtight" style="margin-right: 0.1952em;">
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    L
                   </span>
                   <span class="mopen mtight">
                    (
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0269em;">
                    w
                   </span>
                   <span class="mclose mtight">

    <h2>
     <a id="26N_x1_x2_ldots_xN__mathcalNmu_sigma2_mu__muMLE___mu__mathcalNmu_0_sigma_02_muMAP___142">
     </a>
     2-6假设有N个样本
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        x 
         
         
         
           ( 
          
         
           1 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          x 
         
         
         
           ( 
          
         
           2 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
       
         , 
        
       
         … 
        
       
         , 
        
        
        
          x 
         
         
         
           ( 
          
         
           N 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
       
      
        x^{(1)}, x^{(2)}, \ldots, x^{(N)}
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0824em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mopen mtight">
                  (
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  1
                 </span>
                 <span class="mclose mtight">
                  )
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="mord">
          <span class="mord mathnormal">
           x
          </span>
          <span class="msupsub">
           <span class="vlist-t">
            <span class="vlist-r">
             <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;">
              <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
               <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
               </span>
               <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                <span class="mord mtight">
                 <span class="mopen mtight">
                  (
                 </span>
                 <span class="mord mtight">
                  2
                 </span>
                 <span class="mclose mtight">
                  )
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
         <span class="mpunct">
          ,
         </span>
         <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
         </span>
         <span class="minner">
          …
         </span>

            ) 
           
          
            2 
           
          
         
        
          \ln L(\mu) = -\frac{N}{2}\ln(2\pi\sigma^2) - \frac{1}{2\sigma^2}\sum_{n=1}^N(x^{(n)}-\mu)^2
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">

           <span class="mclose">

           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">

           </span>

           </span>
          </span>

       求导并令其为0：
       <br/>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">

          \frac{\partial \ln L(\mu)}{\partial \mu} = \frac{1}{\sigma^2}\sum_{n=1}^N(x^{(n)}-\mu) = 0

      <p>
       解得：
       <br/>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">

            x 
           
           
           
             ( 
            
           
             n 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
        
          \mu^{MLE} = \frac{1}{N}\sum_{n=1}^N x^{(n)}
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0358em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">

                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    n
                   </span>
                   <span class="mrel mtight">
                    =
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mtight">

                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.2029em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">
                   N
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">

               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.2997em;">

                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathnormal">
             x
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.888em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">

                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mopen mtight">

                   </span>

         </span>

       </span>
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     (2) 最大后验估计(MAP)：
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       根据贝叶斯定理，后验概率正比于似然函数与先验概率的乘积：
       <br/>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          p 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           μ 
          
         
           ∣ 
          
         
           X 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           ∝ 
          
         
           p 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           X 
          
         
           ∣ 
          
         
           μ 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           p 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           μ 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
          p(\mu|X) \propto p(X|\mu)p(\mu)
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">

           <span class="mord mathnormal">

           </span>
           <span class="mopen">

           </span>

           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            ∣
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">

           <span class="mclose">

           <span class="mrel">
            ∝
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            p
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">

           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            ∣
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">

           </span>
           <span class="mclose">

           </span>

           </span>

           </span>

     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       求导并令其为0：
       <br/>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          ∂ 
            
           
             ln 
            
           
             ⁡ 
            
           
             p 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             μ 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             X 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
           
           
             ∂ 
            
           
             μ 
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
          
          
            1 
           
           
           
             σ 
            
           
             2 
            
           
          
          
          
            ∑ 
           
           
           
             n 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            N 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
          
          
            x 
           
           
           
             ( 
            
           
             n 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
           − 
          
         
           μ 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           − 
          
          
           
           
             μ 
            
           
             − 
            
            
            
              μ 
             
            
              0 
             
            
           
           
           
             σ 
            
           
             0 
            
           
             2 
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          \frac{\partial \ln p(\mu|X)}{\partial \mu} = \frac{1}{\sigma^2}\sum_{n=1}^N(x^{(n)}-\mu) - \frac{\mu-\mu_0}{\sigma_0^2} = 0
         </span>

                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;">
                        <span class="">
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">

               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.5916em;">
                <span class="">

              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="mclose nulldelimiter">

          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h2>
     <a id="27NMAPMLE_173">
     </a>
     2-7证明在上一题中，当N趋近于无穷时，最大后验估计(MAP)趋向于最大似然估计(MLE)。
    </h2>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       回顾两个估计的结果：
      </p>
      <p>
       MLE:
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          μ 
           
           
           
             M 
            
           
             L 
            
           
             E 
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
          
          
            1 
           
          
            N 
           
          
          
          
            ∑ 
           
           
           
             n 
            
           
             = 
            
           
             1 
            
           
          
            N 
           
          
          
          
            x 
           
           
           
             ( 
            
           
             n 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
        
          \mu^{MLE} = \frac{1}{N}\sum_{n=1}^N x^{(n)}
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.0358em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;">

       MAP:
       <span class="katex--inline">

         <span class="katex-html">

     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       当N趋近于无穷时，分析各项：
      </p>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          lim 
            
           
             ⁡ 
            
           
           
           
             N 
            
           
             → 
            
           
             ∞ 
            
           
          
          
           
           
             σ 
            
           
             0 
            
           
             2 
            
           
           
           
             N 
            
            
            
              σ 
             
            
              0 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             + 
            
            
            
              σ 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
          
           
           
             lim 
            
           
             ⁡ 
            
           
           
           
             N 
            
           
             → 
            
           
             ∞ 
            
           
          
          
          
            1 
           
           
           
             N 
            
           
             + 
            
            
             
             
               σ 
              
             
               2 
              
             
             
             
               σ 
              
             
               0 
              
             
               2 
              
             
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
         
           1 
          
         
        
          \lim_{N \to \infty} \frac{\sigma_0^2}{N\sigma_0^2 + \sigma^2} = \lim_{N \to \infty} \frac{1}{N + \frac{\sigma^2}{\sigma_0^2}} = 1
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.7258em; vertical-align: -0.5916em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mop">
            <span class="mop">
             lim
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">

          lim

               σ

               σ 
              
             
               0 
              
             
               2 
              
             
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          \lim_{N \to \infty} \frac{\sigma^2}{N\sigma_0^2 + \sigma^2} = \lim_{N \to \infty} \frac{\frac{\sigma^2}{\sigma_0^2}}{N + \frac{\sigma^2}{\sigma_0^2}} = 0

            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t">

                    M
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    L
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0576em;">
                    E
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       直观解释：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        当样本量N很大时，数据提供的信息远多于先验信息
       </li>
       <li>
        先验分布的影响（第二项）趋近于0
       </li>
       <li>
        样本信息的权重（第一项）趋近于1
       </li>
       <li>
        因此MAP估计渐近地等价于MLE估计
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h2>
     <a id="28261_fx__mathbbE_ysim_p_ryxy_201">
     </a>
     2-8验证公式2.61，即证明在平方损失函数下，最优模型为条件期望
     <span class="katex--inline">
      <span class="katex">
       <span class="katex-mathml">
        f 
         
        
          ∗ 
         
        
       
         (

           x 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
        
       
         [ 
        
       
         y 
        
       
         ] 
        
       
      
        f^*(x) = \mathbb{E}_{y\sim p_r(y|x)}[y]
       </span>
       <span class="katex-html">
        <span class="base">
         <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">

    </h2>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       首先回顾期望误差的定义（公式2.60）：
      </p>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          R 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           f 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           = 
          
          
          
            E 
           
           
           
             ( 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             , 
            
           
             y 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
             ∼ 
            
            
            
              p 
             
            
              r 
             
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             , 
            
           
             y 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
           [ 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           y 
          
         
           − 
          
         
           f 
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           ) 
          
          
          
            ) 
           
          
            2 
           
          
         
           ] 
          
         
        
          \mathcal{R}(f) = \mathbb{E}_{(x,y)\sim p_r(x,y)}[(y - f(x))^2]
         </span>

     <li>
      <p>
       验证这是最小值而非最大值：
      </p>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          ∂ 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
             R 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             f 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
           
           
             ∂ 
            
           
             f 
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             x 
            
            
            
              ) 
             
            
              2 
             
            
           
          
         
           = 
          
         
           2 
          
         
           &gt; 
          
         
           0 
          
         
        
          \frac{\partial^2 \mathcal{R}(f|x)}{\partial f(x)^2} = 2 &gt; 0
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.6289em; vertical-align: -0.52em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mopen nulldelimiter">
            </span>
            <span class="mfrac">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 1.1089em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.655em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0556em;">
                    ∂
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
                    f
                   </span>
                   <span class="mopen mtight">
                    (
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    x
                   </span>
                   <span class="mclose mtight">
                    <span class="mclose mtight">
                     )
                    </span>
                    <span class="msupsub">
                     <span class="vlist-t">
                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.7463em;">
                        <span class="" style="top: -2.786em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                         <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                         </span>
                         <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                          <span class="mord mtight">
                           2
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.23em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="frac-line" style="border-bottom-width: 0.04em;">
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span class="" style="top: -3.485em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 3em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    <span class="mord mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0556em;">
                     ∂
                    </span>
                    <span class="msupsub">
                     <span class="vlist-t">
                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.8913em;">
                        <span class="" style="top: -2.931em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                         <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                         </span>
                         <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                          <span class="mord mtight">
                           2
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathcal mtight">
                    R
                   </span>
                   <span class="mopen mtight">
                    (
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
                    f
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    ∣
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    x
                   </span>
                   <span class="mclose mtight">
                    )
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.52em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
            <span class="mclose nulldelimiter">
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            =
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6835em; vertical-align: -0.0391em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            2
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            &gt;
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            0
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       因此对每个x，最优预测为：
      </p>
      <p>
       <span class="katex--inline">
        <span class="katex">
         <span class="katex-mathml">
          f 
           
          
            ∗ 
           
          
         
           ( 
          
         
           x 
          
         
           ) 
          
         
           = 
          
          
          
            E 
           
           
           
             y 
            
           
             ∼ 
            
            
            
              p 
             
            
              r 
             
            
           
             ( 
            
           
             y 
            
           
             ∣ 
            
           
             x 
            
           
             ) 
            
           
          
         
           [ 
          
         
           y 
          
         
           ] 
          
         
        
          f^*(x) = \mathbb{E}_{y\sim p_r(y|x)}[y]
         </span>
         <span class="katex-html">
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">
             f
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6887em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mbin mtight">
                   ∗
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            (
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal">
            x
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            )
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mrel">
            =
           </span>
           <span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;">
           </span>
          </span>
          <span class="base">
           <span class="strut" style="height: 1.1052em; vertical-align: -0.3552em;">
           </span>
           <span class="mord">
            <span class="mord mathbb">
             E
            </span>
            <span class="msupsub">
             <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3448em;">
                <span class="" style="top: -2.5198em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;">
                 <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;">
                 </span>
                 <span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight">
                  <span class="mord mtight">
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                    y
                   </span>
                   <span class="mrel mtight">
                    ∼
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                     p
                    </span>
                    <span class="msupsub">
                     <span class="vlist-t vlist-t2">
                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1645em;">
                        <span class="" style="top: -2.357em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.0714em;">
                         <span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;">
                         </span>
                         <span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight">
                          <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">
                           r
                          </span>
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span class="vlist-s">
                        ​
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span class="vlist-r">
                       <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.143em;">
                        <span class="">
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <span class="mopen mtight">
                    (
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
                    y
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mtight">
                    ∣
                   </span>
                   <span class="mord mathnormal mtight">
                    x
                   </span>
                   <span class="mclose mtight">
                    )
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </span>
               </span>
               <span class="vlist-s">
                ​
               </span>
              </span>
              <span class="vlist-r">
               <span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3552em;">
                <span class="">
                </span>
               </span>
              </span>
             </span>
            </span>
           </span>
           <span class="mopen">
            [
           </span>
           <span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0359em;">
            y
           </span>
           <span class="mclose">
            ]
           </span>
          </span>
         </span>
        </span>
       </span>
      </p>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h2>
     <a id="211_231">
     </a>
     2-11分别用一元、二元和三元特征的词袋模型表示文本"我打了张三"和"张三打了我"，并分析不同模型的优缺点。
    </h2>
    <ol>
     <li>
      一元特征(Unigram)表示：
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     文本分词后：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      句子1：“我”，“打”，“了”，“张三”
     </li>
     <li>
      句子2：“张三”，“打”，“了”，“我”
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     特征词典：{“我”, “打”, “了”, “张三”}
    </p>
    <p>
     向量表示：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      句子1：[1, 1, 1, 1]
     </li>
     <li>
      句子2：[1, 1, 1, 1]
     </li>
    </ul>
    <ol start="2">
     <li>
      二元特征(Bigram)表示：
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     特征词典：{“我打”, “打了”, “了张三”, “张三打”, “打了”, “了我”}
    </p>
    <p>
     向量表示：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      句子1：[1, 1, 1, 0, 0, 0]
     </li>
     <li>
      句子2：[0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 1]
     </li>
    </ul>
    <ol start="3">
     <li>
      三元特征(Trigram)表示：
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     特征词典：{“我打了”, “打了张三”, “了张三”, “张三打了”, “三打了我”}
    </p>
    <p>
     向量表示：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      句子1：[1, 1, 0, 0, 0]
     </li>
     <li>
      句子2：[0, 0, 0, 1, 1]
     </li>
    </ul>
    <ol>
     <li>
      一元特征模型：
      <br/>
      优点：
     </li>
    </ol>
    <ul>
     <li>
      特征空间较小，计算效率高
     </li>
     <li>
      对数据稀疏性不敏感
     </li>
     <li>
      词序无关的场景下表现好
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     缺点：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      完全丢失词序信息
     </li>
     <li>
      无法区分语义相反的句子
     </li>
     <li>
      如本例中无法区分主谓关系
     </li>
    </ul>
    <ol start="2">
     <li>
      二元特征模型：
      <br/>
      优点：
     </li>
    </ol>
    <ul>
     <li>
      保留了部分相邻词的顺序信息
     </li>
     <li>
      能够捕捉一定的短语特征
     </li>
     <li>
      可以区分简单的语序差异
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     缺点：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      特征空间显著增大
     </li>
     <li>
      数据稀疏性问题加重
     </li>
     <li>
      只能捕获局部的序列关系
     </li>
    </ul>
    <ol start="3">
     <li>
      三元特征模型：
      <br/>
      优点：
     </li>
    </ol>
    <ul>
     <li>
      保留了更多的上下文信息
     </li>
     <li>
      能够捕捉更长的短语特征
     </li>
     <li>
      语序表达更准确
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     缺点：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      特征空间急剧膨胀
     </li>
     <li>
      严重的数据稀疏问题
     </li>
     <li>
      计算复杂度高
     </li>
     <li>
      泛化能力下降
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h2>
     <a id="212__293">
     </a>
     2-12 计算三分类问题的各项评估指标。
    </h2>
    <p>
     真实标签：1,1,2,2,2,3,3,3,3
     <br/>
     预测标签：1,2,2,2,3,3,3,1,2
     <br/>
     分别计算模型的精确率、召回率、F1值以及它们的宏平均和微平均。
    </p>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <p>
       首先构建混淆矩阵：
       <br/>
       预测\真实 类别1 类别2 类别3
       <br/>
       类别1 1 0 1
       <br/>
       类别2 1 3 1
       <br/>
       类别3 0 0 2
      </p>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       计算每个类别的精确率(Precision)：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        P1 = 1/(1+0+1) = 1/2 = 0.5
       </li>
       <li>
        P2 = 3/(1+3+1) = 3/5 = 0.6
       </li>
       <li>
        P3 = 2/(0+0+2) = 2/2 = 1.0
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       计算每个类别的召回率(Recall)：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        R1 = 1/(1+1+0) = 1/2 = 0.5
       </li>
       <li>
        R2 = 3/(0+3+0) = 3/3 = 1.0
       </li>
       <li>
        R3 = 2/(1+1+2) = 2/4 = 0.5
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       计算每个类别的F1值：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        F1_1 = 2×0.5×0.5/(0.5+0.5) = 0.5
       </li>
       <li>
        F1_2 = 2×0.6×1.0/(0.6+1.0) = 0.75
       </li>
       <li>
        F1_3 = 2×1.0×0.5/(1.0+0.5) = 0.67
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       计算宏平均(Macro-average)：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        Macro-P = (0.5 + 0.6 + 1.0)/3 = 0.70
       </li>
       <li>
        Macro-R = (0.5 + 1.0 + 0.5)/3 = 0.67
       </li>
       <li>
        Macro-F1 = (0.5 + 0.75 + 0.67)/3 = 0.64
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
     <li>
      <p>
       计算微平均(Micro-average)：
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        总TP = 1 + 3 + 2 = 6
       </li>
       <li>
        总样本数 = 9
       </li>
       <li>
        Micro-P = 6/9 = 0.67
       </li>
       <li>
        Micro-R = 6/9 = 0.67
       </li>
       <li>
        Micro-F1 = 2×0.67×0.67/(0.67+0.67) = 0.67
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ol>
    <p>
     类别1：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      Precision = 0.50
     </li>
     <li>
      Recall = 0.50
     </li>
     <li>
      F1 = 0.50
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     类别2：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      Precision = 0.60
     </li>
     <li>
      Recall = 1.00
     </li>
     <li>
      F1 = 0.75
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     类别3：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      Precision = 1.00
     </li>
     <li>
      Recall = 0.50
     </li>
     <li>
      F1 = 0.67
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     宏平均：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      Macro-Precision = 0.70
     </li>
     <li>
      Macro-Recall = 0.67
     </li>
     <li>
      Macro-F1 = 0.64
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     微平均：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      Micro-Precision = 0.67
     </li>
     <li>
      Micro-Recall = 0.67
     </li>
     <li>
      Micro-F1 = 0.67
     </li>
    </ul>
